class=\"infobox-header wiki-backgroundcolor-light\">Upcoming Matches</div></div></div></div>\n<p><b>RLCS Season X </b> is the second <a href=\"/rocketleague/RLCS\" class=\"mw-redirect\" title=\"RLCS\">RLCS</a> season in 2020, crossing over into 2021. This season introduces the most major changes to the RLCS system yet with League Play and bi-annual seasons being abandoned, replaced with an open circuit. 3 splits - Fall, Winter, Spring - each have 3 regional events leading into an international major. Within all these events, each team collects points that will determine whether they will qualify for the World Championship.\n</p>\n<div id=\"toc\" class=\"toc\" role=\"navigation\" href=\"/rocketleague/index.php?title=Rocket_League_Championship_Series/Season_X/Spring/Oceania&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5\" title=\"Edit section: Format\">edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li><b>Group Stage</b> - <i>May 1st</i>\n<ul><li>10 teams - split into 2 groups of 5.</li>\n<li>Round Robin <abbr title=\"Best of 5\">Bo5</abbr>\n<ul><li>Tiebreakers:\n<ul><li>In the case of a tie, game differential is the primary tiebreaker that seeds the teams, followed by Head to Head.</li></ul></li></ul></li>\n<li><span style=\"background-color:rgb(221,244,221);\">Top four </span> of each group advance to the <a href=\"#Playoffs\">Playoffs</a>.</li>\n<li><span style=\"background-color:rgb(251,223,223);\">5th place</span> of each group is eliminated.<br /><br /></li></ul></li>\n<li><b>Playoffs</b> - <i>May 2nd</i>\n<ul><li>Single Elimination Bracket.\n<ul><li>All matches are <abbr title=\"Best of 7\">Bo7</abbr>.</li></ul></li></ul></li></ul>\n<h3><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Prize_Pool\">Prize Pool</span><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a
